static method computeLinkStats({required lin::LinkTable linkTable, required sna3::SnapshotAnalysis base, required sna3::SnapshotAnalysis patch}) → lin2::LinkSuccessEvent {
  final core::List<sna3::Code> baseCodes = base.{sna3::SnapshotAnalysis::functions}{core::List<sna3::Code>}.{core::Iterable::toList}(){({growable: core::bool}) → core::List<sna3::Code>};
  final core::List<sna3::Code> patchCodes = patch.{sna3::SnapshotAnalysis::functions}{core::List<sna3::Code>}.{core::Iterable::toList}(){({growable: core::bool}) → core::List<sna3::Code>};
